) } // Histogram Chart const HistogramChart = ({ data, bins = 10, size = { width: 300, height: 200 } }: { data: number[]; bins?: number; size?: { width: number; height: number } }) => { const padding = 40 const chartWidth = size.width - padding * 2, chartHeight = size.height - padding * 2 const min = Math.min(...data), max = Math.max(...data) const binWidth = (max - min) / bins const histogram: { range: string; count: number; color: string }[] = [] for (let i = 0; i < bins; i++) { const start = min + i * binWidth, end = start + binWidth const count = data.filter(v => v >= start && (i === bins - 1 ? v <= end : v < end)).length histogram.push({ range: `${start.toFixed(1)}`, count, color: `hsl(${260 + i * 20}, 70%, 60%)` }) } const maxCount = Math.max(...histogram.map(h => h.count), 1) return (
) } // Waterfall Chart const WaterfallChart = ({ data, size = { width: 300, height: 220 } }: { data: { label: string; value: number; color?: string }[]; size?: { width: number; height: number } }) => { const padding = 40 const chartWidth = size.width - padding * 2, chartHeight = size.height - padding * 2 - 20 // Use reduce to avoid reassignment const processedData = data.reduce<{ label: string; value: number; start: number; end: number; isPositive: boolean; color?: string }[]>((acc, item, i) => { const start = i === 0 ? 0 : acc[i - 1].end const end = start + item.value acc.push({ ...item, start, end, isPositive: item.value >= 0 }) return acc }, []) const maxValue = Math.max(...processedData.map(d => Math.abs(d.end)), ...processedData.map(d => Math.abs(d.start)), 1) const barWidth = chartWidth / data.length * 0.7 return (
) } // Sunburst Chart const SunburstChart = ({ data, size = 180 }: { data: { label: string; value: number; color: string; children?: { label: string; value: number; color: string }[] }[]; size?: number }) => { const total = data.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.value, 0) const centerX = size / 2, centerY = size / 2 const innerRadius = size / 6, outerRadius = size / 2 - 10 const middleRadius = (innerRadius + outerRadius) / 2 const segments: { startAngle: number; endAngle: number; color: string; label: string; value: number; inner: number; outer: number }[] = [] let currentAngle = -90 data.forEach(item => { const angle = (item.value / total) * 360 segments.push({ startAngle: currentAngle, endAngle: currentAngle + angle, color: item.color, label: item.label, value: item.value, inner: innerRadius, outer: middleRadius - 2 }) if (item.children) { const childTotal = item.children.reduce((s, c) => s + c.value, 0) let childAngle = currentAngle item.children.forEach(child => { const cAngle = (child.value / childTotal) * angle segments.push({ startAngle: childAngle, endAngle: childAngle + cAngle, color: child.color, label: child.label, value: child.value, inner: middleRadius + 2, outer: outerRadius }) childAngle += cAngle }) } currentAngle += angle }) return (
{data.map((item, i) => (
{item.label}
))}
